Moved Files:
------------
Android Gradle projects use a different directory structure than ADT
Eclipse projects. Here's how the projects were restructured:

* AndroidManifest.xml => app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml
* res/ => app/src/main/res/
* src/ => app/src/main/java/
* src/com/android/settings/EventLogTags.logtags => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/EventLogTags.logtags
* src/com/android/settings/accessibility/OWNERS => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/accessibility/OWNERS
* src/com/android/settings/applications/appinfo/OWNERS => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/applications/appinfo/OWNERS
* src/com/android/settings/applications/assist/OWNERS => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/applications/assist/OWNERS
* src/com/android/settings/applications/autofill/OWNERS => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/applications/autofill/OWNERS
* src/com/android/settings/applications/specialaccess/notificationaccess/OWNERS => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/applications/specialaccess/notificationaccess/OWNERS
* src/com/android/settings/applications/specialaccess/zenaccess/OWNERS => app/src/main/resources/com/android/settings/applications/specialaccess/zenaccess/OWNERS

Next Steps:
-----------
You can now build the project. The Gradle project needs network
connectivity to download dependencies.

Bugs:
-----
If for some reason your project does not build, and you determine that
it is due to a bug or limitation of the Eclipse to Gradle importer,
please file a bug at http://b.android.com with category
Component-Tools.

(This import summary is for your information only, and can be deleted
after import once you are satisfied with the results.)
